# 宠物美术资源提示词清单（282只 × 4张 = 1128张）

---

## 一、通用 Prompt 前缀（4种图共4个前缀）

### 前缀A：普通形态全身图（normal_full）
```
chibi 2D Chinese ink wash painting game character, super deformed cute style, big head small body ratio 2:1, Chinese calligraphy brush-style black ink outlines with varying thickness and brush stroke feel, ink wash coloring with subtle ink wash gradation within same color tone, rich traditional Chinese mineral pigment colors (vermilion cinnabar red, azurite blue, malachite green, ochre yellow, ink black), Chinese Xianxia mythology aesthetic, NOT Western fantasy, NOT realistic, NOT 3D, full body view front-facing centered on canvas, solid plain single-color background light gray #E0E0E0, expressive ink-painted eyes, game asset style, clean sharp ink-line edges for easy cutout. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: any text, any letters, any characters, any words, any writing, any labels, any captions, any watermark, any signature. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: white outline outside black ink outlines, white border around character, white edge glow, white halo, any white fringe between character outline and background, any color bleeding outside the black ink outlines. The black ink outline must be the absolute outermost edge directly touching the background with zero gap. Also forbidden: glow effects, blur, soft edges, lighting effects. This is the NORMAL base form (not evolved).
```

### 前缀B：普通形态头像（normal_avatar）
```
chibi 2D Chinese ink wash painting game character icon, super deformed cute style, big head small body ratio 2:1, Chinese calligraphy brush-style black ink outlines with varying thickness and brush stroke feel, ink wash coloring with subtle ink wash gradation within same color tone, rich traditional Chinese mineral pigment colors (vermilion cinnabar red, azurite blue, malachite green, ochre yellow, ink black), Chinese Xianxia mythology aesthetic, NOT Western fantasy, NOT realistic, NOT 3D, square 1:1 aspect ratio, close-up showing oversized head and upper shoulders, solid plain single-color background light gray #E0E0E0, expressive ink-painted eyes, game icon style, clean sharp ink-line edges for easy cutout. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: any text, any letters, any characters, any words, any writing, any labels, any captions, any watermark, any signature. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: white outline outside black ink outlines, white border around character, white edge glow, white halo, any white fringe between character outline and background, any color bleeding outside the black ink outlines. The black ink outline must be the absolute outermost edge directly touching the background with zero gap. Also forbidden: glow effects, blur, soft edges, lighting effects. This is the NORMAL base form (not evolved).
```

### 前缀C：觉醒形态全身图（awakened_full）
```
chibi 2D Chinese ink wash painting game character, super deformed cute style, big head small body ratio 2:1, Chinese calligraphy brush-style black ink outlines with varying thickness and brush stroke feel, ink wash coloring with subtle ink wash gradation within same color tone, rich traditional Chinese mineral pigment colors (vermilion cinnabar red, azurite blue, malachite green, ochre yellow, ink black), Chinese Xianxia mythology aesthetic with more ornate decorations and spirit runes and flowing ribbons and Daoist symbols, NOT Western fantasy, NOT realistic, NOT 3D, full body view front-facing centered on canvas, solid plain single-color background light gray #E0E0E0, expressive ink-painted eyes, game asset style, clean sharp ink-line edges for easy cutout, more refined details decorations and accessories than base version, golden star-rank accents on key accessories to signify max rank. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: any text, any letters, any characters, any words, any writing, any labels, any captions, any watermark, any signature. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: white outline outside black ink outlines, white border around character, white edge glow, white halo, any white fringe between character outline and background, any color bleeding outside the black ink outlines. The black ink outline must be the absolute outermost edge directly touching the background with zero gap. Also forbidden: glow effects, blur, soft edges, lighting effects.
```

### 前缀D：觉醒形态头像（awakened_avatar）
```
chibi 2D Chinese ink wash painting game character icon, super deformed cute style, big head small body ratio 2:1, Chinese calligraphy brush-style black ink outlines with varying thickness and brush stroke feel, ink wash coloring with subtle ink wash gradation within same color tone, rich traditional Chinese mineral pigment colors (vermilion cinnabar red, azurite blue, malachite green, ochre yellow, ink black), Chinese Xianxia mythology aesthetic with more ornate decorations and spirit runes and flowing ribbons and Daoist symbols, NOT Western fantasy, NOT realistic, NOT 3D, square 1:1 aspect ratio, close-up showing oversized head and upper shoulders, solid plain single-color background light gray #E0E0E0, expressive ink-painted eyes, game icon style, clean sharp ink-line edges for easy cutout, more refined details decorations and accessories than base version, golden star-rank accents on key accessories to signify max rank. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: any text, any letters, any characters, any words, any writing, any labels, any captions, any watermark, any signature. STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: white outline outside black ink outlines, white border around character, white edge glow, white halo, any white fringe between character outline and background, any color bleeding outside the black ink outlines. The black ink outline must be the absolute outermost edge directly touching the background with zero gap. Also forbidden: glow effects, blur, soft edges, lighting effects.
```

### 拼接方式
完整 prompt = `{前缀} + {角色特征描述}` + 分辨率后缀

- 全身图后缀：`Resolution: 512x512px target, the character should fill about 70-80% of the canvas height.`
- 头像后缀：`Resolution: 128x128px target, circular crop friendly composition.`

### 文件命名规范
- `{pet_id}_normal_full.png` — 普通形态全身
- `{pet_id}_normal_avatar.png` — 普通形态头像
- `{pet_id}_awakened_full.png` — 觉醒形态全身
- `{pet_id}_awakened_avatar.png` — 觉醒形态头像
- `{pet_id}_normal_full_nobg.png` — 普通全身抠图版
- `{pet_id}_awakened_full_nobg.png` — 觉醒全身抠图版

存放目录：`assets/pets_gen/`

---

## 二、宠物角色特征描述

> 下表中每只宠物包含4条角色特征描述，分别对应4种图片类型。
> 完整 prompt = 对应前缀 + 角色特征描述 + 分辨率后缀

### 兽灵族（52只）

#### 火狐（fire_fox）— R 火 兽灵族

**A. 普通全身（normal_full）角色描述：**
```
A young fox spirit in battle-ready base form, orange-gold fur rendered in flowing ink wash brush strokes, large bright teal eyes with sharp determined battle gaze, pointed ears alert and angled back, a single fluffy tail raised and bristling with fighting spirit, wearing a simple vermilion red silk ribbon collar, front paws spread in a low aggressive combat stance ready to pounce, body slightly crouched and leaning forward, mouth slightly open showing tiny fangs in a fierce growl, energetic and feisty expression.
```

**B. 普通头像（normal_avatar）角色描述：**
```
A young fox spirit in battle-ready base form,  orange-gold fur rendered in flowing ink wash brush strokes,  large bright teal eyes with sharp determined battle gaze,  pointed ears alert and angled back,  a single fluffy tail raised and bristling with fighting spirit,  wearing a simple vermilion red silk ribbon collar.
```

**C. 觉醒全身（awakened_full）角色描述：**
```
A fire fox spirit in max-star evolved form mid-battle, vibrant orange-gold fur in flowing ink wash with brush stroke texture, sharp intelligent teal eyes blazing with golden star ring and fierce battle spirit, pointed ears with elaborate red flame tips and golden earring ornaments angled back aggressively, ornate red jade fire pendant with golden Daoist flame rune swinging with movement, dynamic leaping attack pose with one front paw swiping forward showing claws, body twisting mid-strike with powerful momentum, bushy golden-tipped red tail fanned out behind in combat stance, mouth open in a battle cry showing fangs, intense warrior expression mixing cunning and ferocity, golden fire-fox spirit runes trailing from the swiping paw.
```

**D. 觉醒头像（awakened_avatar）角色描述：**
```
A fire fox spirit in max-star evolved form, vibrant orange-gold fur in flowing ink wash with brush stroke texture,  sharp intelligent teal eyes blazing with golden star ring and fierce battle spirit,  pointed ears with elaborate red flame tips and golden earring ornaments angled back aggressively,  ornate red jade fire pendant with golden Daoist flame rune swinging with movement,  dynamic leaping attack pose with one front paw swiping forward showing claws,  body twisting mid-strike with powerful momentum.
```
